        <div class="cell destinationreview"></div>                    <div id="parent2336651" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2336651" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="valkyriee"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2053372"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2053372.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="valkyriee" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2336651ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2336651" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2053372">valkyriee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-03"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730648415" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Smells like a very fresh, juicy, slightly sour mango in the very beginning. Nothing too special? Or definitely too hyped. <br />
<br />
The magic happens in the drydown for me. It has to be the ginger and musk, that gives this scent a little bit more layers, that I enjoy.<br />
<br />
That's about it. Considering the hype about it, it's just alright. Not terribly bad, not mind-blowingly good either.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2336651"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2336651#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2334824" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2059233">vinky</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-24">09/24/24 01:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ginger and mango take center stage for a vibrant opening. The ginger provides a spicy brightness, but it fades quickly, allowing the mango to shine through as it quickly transitions from a slightly green, underripe scent to something more lush, sweet, and juicy. I usually avoid red berry notes in fragrances, as they can sometimes smell overly sweet in an oddly hollow way or artificial, but here they seem to enhance the mango, giving it a more natural, juicy quality rather than a synthetic candy-like impression. The lemon adds a zesty freshness that is present, but doesn't overpower and pull the fragrance into a citrus territory. <br />
<br />
The cedar then comes into play, welcoming some earthiness and easing in the transition to the fragrance‚Äôs amber-y, musky base. There‚Äôs a subtle warmth from the amber and coumarin that pairs well with the musk, though the synthetic nature of the musk becomes more apparent as the scent develops. The oud adds depth, but doesn't gain prominence until we've really gotten to the base. <br />
<br />
Overall, God of Fire is pleasant. Given the amount of buzz surrounding this scent, I was expecting something a bit more refined or memorable. It‚Äôs enjoyable for what it is‚Äîan amber-y, musky oud with a fun, fruity initial spray‚Äîbut I don't find the mango to be particularly convincing or the base to be unlike any other amber or fresh-leaning oud, though I admit I'm not super experienced with the category. <br />
<br />
Won't be seeking any more of it, but it was a fun experience!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2293242"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2293242#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2289133" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Maybe it‚Äôs the sleek and stunning design of the bottles, or perhaps it‚Äôs my fascination with snakes.  Or possibly, my complete adoration for Mortal Skin has just bought me a lot of goodwill for the brand.<br />
<br />
But I finally got my hands on a sample of God of Fire, and I was‚Ä¶disappointed.<br />
<br />
Like everyone else with an internet connection, I had heard the hype around this fragrance.  Apparently, TikTok (the dumbing down of society) has been hyping and fanning the flames around God of Fire, particularly with teenage boys.  And might I say, I find the thought of teenagers gleefully spraying and tossing around $230.00 bottles of St√©phane Humbert Lucas 777 in the locker room after gym class to be absolutely hysterical.<br />
<br />
To be honest, I probably would‚Äôve thought this scent was the shit in high school, too, because a mango-based fragrance geared toward men would‚Äôve seemed revolutionary in the 2000s.  I probably would‚Äôve also liked mango martinis at that time, too, and this fragrance reeks of a fruity, tropical, hyper-sweet and diabetes-inducing mango-tini that you just accidentally dropped in your lap.<br />
<br />
But as an adult who rolls his eyes at TikTok and is only a few years away from snarling at kids to get off his lawn, I find God of Fire to be somewhat immature, underdeveloped and, frankly, overhyped.  Supposedly, there‚Äôs additional notes of ginger, lemon, musk, and red berries.  I can maybe (barely) detect those red berries, but otherwise this is just a straight shot of unnuanced mango.  Nothing more, nothing less.<br />
<br />
In five words of less: Leave this one for TikTok.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2274264"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2274264#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2272308" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2233131"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2233131#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2231725" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2231725" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JusttheFactsMan"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1733487.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JusttheFactsMan" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Arte-Profumi/Ecclesiae-20783.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.20783.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ecclesiae"title="Ecclesiae"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2231725ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2231725" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487">JusttheFactsMan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-28">07/28/24 07:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>#767 in my "Tour de Fragrance"<br />
<br />
Another user asked my opinion of Maison Alhambra Malachite as a clone of either Le Gemme Kobraa or Humbert God of Fire, and I had planned to buy Malachite. Got it yesterday and I'm comparing it to sprayettes of Kobraa and God of Fire from FragranceLine. <br />
<br />
So about God of Fire specifically. It is a lovely scent. In my mind I was hearing that song "Underneath the Mango Tree" from the James Bond Film, "Dr. No." It's more tropical and unisex, even feminine, than either Le Gemme Kobraa or Sceptre Malachite. Admittedly I'm a fan of the tropical Jean Paul Gaultier scents, though not a fan of their performance. So if Humbert tossed some coconut into this scent I might lose my mind and buy a full bottle.<br />
<br />
Now on to the controversy with the crowds out there insisting Maison Alhambra's Malachite is a clone of Kobraa and those insisting it's a clone God of Fire. It's closer to God of Fire, but definitely not a clone of either. You can get samples of both from FragrancesLine like I did, compare them to Malachite, which you should absolutely buy, and smell for yourself. The openings of Kobraa and Malachite are close enough I wasn't sure if I was imagining a difference or not. But there's definitely a difference in the openings you will notice but could talk yourself into ignoring. Not so five minutes later. That's when the fruitiness of the Malachite comes out, which is why the "God of Fire" guys are sweating with excitement. But it's citrus and currants, not mangoes and berries. GOF is a touch more beach wear than Malachite, and feminine enough that I may get a bottle for a girlfriend, but probably not for myself. <br />
<br />
One caveat here is that simple formula, wood-focused scents like Kobraa will always outlast complex, more fruit-focused scents like God of Fire and Malachite. The molecular nature of fruit scents provides strong initial projection that disappears relatively soon in the evolution of the scent on our skin. The lemon, tangerine, grapefruit, mango, pineapple, currants, berries, all ephemeral. Woods last all day long. So Kobraa will get through the work day. God of Fire and Malachite barely make it to lunch. I find having to respray midday annoying and often utterly inconvenient if not impossible. It's why I abandoned Colognes and Eau de Toilettes and seldom buy them no matter how much I like them.<br />
<br />
That said guys, the Malachite is dirt cheap at $23 and close enough to Kobraa and God of Fire to make fans of both happy. So I'm glad I bought a bottle of Malachite and samples of GOF and Kobraa instead of dropping the price of a car payment for full bottles of Kobraa or God of Fire. My recommendation is just get the Malachite and be happy. And I will repeat all this in separate reviews on the Malachite and of Kobraa pages. Unless money is no issue, in which case I'd get all three.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2231725"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2231725#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2230958" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2148915">Bread6602</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-13">07/13/24 22:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There is a lot of hype around this fragrance. I was looking forward to trying it. When I ordered a sample and tried it I was a little let down. However, as I wore the fragrance for a couple weeks I grew to love it. <br />
<br />
I always see people talking about the mango note. I do not get a strong mango note. To me the mango mixes with the red berries and floral notes to make a very tropical and slightly woody scent. I was expecting a front and center mango note like one featured in Mind Games Blockade. I think it is completely unisex but might lean slightly feminine. However, my girlfriend says it is differently a masculine scent. This is probably cause my definition of a masculine scent would be Creed Aventus or PDM Haltane. <br />
<br />
I see mixed reviews about the performance. For me it has very good longevity and projection. Easily 12+ hours of longevity with 6+ hours of great projection. It really just depends on your skin composition. <br />
<br />
Longevity: 10/10<br />
Projection: 9/10<br />
Smell: 9/10<br />
Price: 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2218008"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2218008#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2215419" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2201788" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="yrogovich"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1759676"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1759676.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="yrogovich" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2201788ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2201788" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1759676">yrogovich</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-28">06/28/24 03:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance has been my companion since last summer. A delightful tropical mango (quite rare note in perfumes), devoid of artificial chemical notes, doesn't overwhelm with its tropical sweetness even in the most sweltering heat. A subtle hint of ginger adds a touch of spiciness to the scent, making it playful and sexy.<br />
<br />
This was a blind buy purchase and it was a perfect decision. I've discovered that it's perfect for vibrant occasions - concerts, travels, or simply moments when I want to lift my mood. The sillage is exquisite; I often received compliments. Its longevity is impressive - the scent is still noticeable even in the evening.<br />
<br />
It's a unisex fragrance that works well year-round. However, in winter, the ginger note becomes more dominant than the tropical mango. While still wearable, on cold days the scent somewhat "contracts," losing some of its tropical depth.<br />
<br />
Overall, it's a multifaceted, elegant fragrance that especially shines in warmer months, adding a touch of exoticism and positive energy to both everyday and special moments.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It also performs like beast (albeit in that ‚Äúmolecular‚Äù way), and obviously‚Ä¶the bottle is cool af.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2196020"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2196020#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2195829" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2168111">m6nu</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-22">06/22/24 02:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Got really pulled into this due to the presentation and bright blue colour of the bottle, and I am glad it did catch my attention. If you are looking for a summer fragerance, and if you love fruity and tropical scents then this is the one for you. <br />
I do understand why people compare the God of Fire to the Erba Pura (Xerjoff). But having smelt both of them side by side at the start and their dry down. I definitely prefer the God of Fire, and this is why (all the reasons below are subjective and I have compared them on paper and on my my skin):<br />
1. The "fruity" note - God of Fire is pretty much just Mango (maybe hints of passionfruit or pineapple). However Erba Pura is a lot more than just mango and it puts out an extremely fruity scent. If you do prefer very fruity scents, Erba Pura will be the better out of the two. In my opinion Erba Pura is a lot more feminine unisex.<br />
2. Dry down - God of Fire dries down to a lot more amber/woody and musk. It is a lot more soothing, and the projection is not crazy to point where it will be giving headaches to people around you. Erba Pura on the other hand does dry down a lot more powdery and musk like. I was a bit sceptical about the synthetic like smell of Erba Pura, until I actually experienced it. The dry down did put me off a little bit, perhaps it reacts weirdly to my skin. But the next two points are more important.<br />
3. Skin vs Paper - God of Fire does extremely well on my skin compared to the paper strip. The notes are much more prominent on my skin and it does react in a very plesant way. I was a bit underwhelmed by the performance and dry down when it was sprayed on a paper strip. However, Erba Pura performed the same on paper and my skin. The only key difference was the synthetic like smell during the dry down phase of the fragerance on my skin.<br />
4. Any topical and perspiration - God of Fire has a neutral/nil effect on a non-scented fragerance. Meaning, you can use a moisturiser on your skin, spray the fragerance and it will smell exactly like it should. Erba Pura often can react to your moisturiser/lotion and the fragerance chemistry can change up. Giving out a more of a werid tropical and fruity scent. It almost reminded me on the washroom cleaning products that smells like tropical, and it was awfully very similar. Also Erba Pura is terrible if you are someone that perspires a lot, the sweat and humidity can really alter the scent of the fragerance. Although Erba Pura is a "summer" fragerance of sort, it is not recommended for humid places (personally). <br />
<br />
I went to buying either Erba Pura or God of Fire. I was very objective when I went in there and I just wanted the best out of these two. For me personally, God of Fire smells better to my liking, performs better on my skin and overall ticks most the boxes. However it is at a price point of ¬£175, which is a lot of money. I would recommend to pick it up if you can get it between ¬£135 - ¬£150.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2195829"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2195829#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2193793" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Performance: 3/10<br />
Bottle, atomiser, cap: 8/10<br />
Price point: 7/10<br />

It was a toss up between this and Carioca Heart and I wish I went with the latter instead because at least it would‚Äôve been unique to my collection. All of these reviews and not one person has mentioned that this is similar to Bond No 9 Greenwich Village. When I say similar I don‚Äôt mean they smell exactly alike. There are differences. GOH is slightly darker because of the oud &amp; cypriol oil. However, they are both within the same fragrance family of fruity amber scents with that airy quality and in the air they have similar qualities. I don't get a specific fruit in particular, I just smell fruits, musk and amber + oak moss.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2128807"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2128807#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2126634" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1758635">lovasen</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-16">04/16/24 13:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>God of Fire smells great, but it might be a bit overrated. It's a fresh, fun, fruity fragrance with a beautiful mango note, and that mango note lasts through the whole wear of the fragrance. It's not the most complex fragrance, it doesn't smell all that high quality, and the mango smells a bit synthetic. I don't pick up on the oud note, I guess it's lurking in the background to add some depth and darken the scent? <br />
That said, I love wearing this in the summer, and it's all around just a really fun fragrance to wear! For 195‚Ç¨ for 50ml, I'd say it's overpriced for what it is, especially seeing as the mango note does smell a bit synthetic. God of Fire also seems to be getting a lot of hype on social media, and so the fragrance might not be as great as it's made out to be by influencers. Still, I personally really like God of Fire, and look forward to wearing it during the summer!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2126634"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2126634#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2123104" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1867346">rensnaps</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-29">03/29/24 12:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Interesting, I don't often write reviews but I felt as though I need to with this one. This fragrance for me feels alive and in the way that it constantly changes and mutates over time. When I first sprayed this fragrance it was fruity, citrusy, tropical mango but after about 15 minutes the coumarin and woodiness took over intensely and it was more spicy and woody than anything, which although pleasant wasn't really what I was looking for. I was very much hoping for a fruity mango tropical scent, and so this was going to easily be a dud. However, after giving it another 15 minutes on my skin the mango note fought it's way back to the forefront and now it's a mango heavy spicy woody scent. And I find that every time I smell it, different notes are fighting their way to the forefront it's incredibly interesting and always changing. This is the exact opposite of a linear fragrance. Now that it's been about over an hour, it's stayed in that mango first, woody/spicy second state for a while and I'm really enjoying it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It's bright and fresh mango in the opening, that changes to what I'd describe as a fresh musk or light oud.  I'd actually like to smell this on someone else 3 hours into wearing it so see if I can still smell the mango, I can't detect it on myself in the dry down.  Ultimately I chose a different mango fragrance over this one, but this is really nice if you like simple scents. It's too expensive for what it is too.  Masculine men should stay clear of this scent, it really is pretty feminine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2079341"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2079341#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2074560" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
First, the design of this bottle is just wow! This is easily one of the more unique designs with the serpent head while being blue by paying tribute to an Aztec Legend. As a mythology nerd, this was amazing to find out how Stephane got his inspiration for this one!<br />
<br />
Then the fragrance itself. Right when you spray it you get the sweetness from the Mango and the Red Berry and the dry down locking in the fruit and combining the wood to make this ultimate mango scent that is to die for. When I say this is the best tropical fragrance I have smelled, I mean it! This thing is wondrous and if you are a fan of any tropical scent or at the very least mango, then you will love this fragrance! It's a perfect fit for Spring and Summer, it lasts long on my skin, and it smells fantastic through and through. <br />
<br />
Easily one of my favorites I have ever gotten and has been one of my best buys yet<br />
<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2031014"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2031014#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2027681" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1515510">SmellySal</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-07">01/07/24 13:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tried this from a decant because I'm not about to sell my first born for a bottle without trying first, and was surprised by how much this fragrance was not what I expected, and how much I love it. I was expecting a sweet, fruity mango fragrance, but I think this is really an oud leaning woody fragrance with a fruity mango opening. The thing that impressed me though, was how smoothly and masterfully the fragrance fades from one profile to another. The mango is really sweet at first-- almost candylike, or like mango sherbet more than actual fruit. Then the sweetness fades a bit and the fragrance goes from photorealistic mango to smoky sweet woods, then again to a musky oud base which I found to be on the lighter side of oud fragrances. Each transition was as smooth as one color fading into another, and each took me by surprise in the best possible way. Some thoughts that ran through my head included a rough financial calculation of how soon I might be able to get my hands on a bottle of this, and that I might actually be ok with giving up my entire collection for a single bottle of God of Fire. I could not stop smelling myself. Projection was fantastic, my husband said I smelled "rich and cool."</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="2023649"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=2023649#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2018553" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; In any case, I‚Äôm not a fan of oud and fruity notes together. I also hate the white musk that underlines this perfume, Kirke, Erba Pura etc. <br />
<br />
It develops better than it opens for sure. Tropical but not juicy. In fact, the fruits here are more artificial fruit flavouring than actual fruit juice. Think sherbet! There‚Äôs something that evokes a high end vacation which makes me want to revisit this in high heat. It‚Äôs absolutely not worth the pricetag in my opinion, but then again someone into loud Tiz Terenzi-esque DNA might disagree. The performance is really good, it lingers in the air for a super long time. On skin you can expect to smell it until you shower. I THOROUGHLY DISLIKE THIS PERFUME, but I can see how it is appealing to some. The DNA is just not something that agrees with me so sold my bottle and learnt a valuable lesson in not blind-buying.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="1972274"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=1972274#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1969580" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1926519" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="stunna"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1837421"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1837421.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="stunna" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Fragrance-Du-Bois/Lovers-82757.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.82757.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Lovers"title="Lovers"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1926519ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1926519" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1837421">stunna</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-12">09/12/23 20:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I think your expectations and feelings about this perfume will depend on what kind of mango you like and how much youtube you watch. This was the first mango I tried, and at first sniff/couple of wears, I was disappointed. After trying other mango scents, though, I can honestly say this is the best mango scent in my opinion. This is a truly juicy, ripe mango with something tart and heavy in addition. It reminds me of eating mango on the beach on a tropical beach in 90% humidity. It's almost sweaty in how thick and heavy the mango is. After many comparisons and wears, I love it. I've tried Mango Skin (not a mango scent after the first 20 mins), Ylang in Gold (floral bomb, no mango), Fleur et Lait (pretty good but linear), and Cruz Del Sur II (just fine, didn't wow me.) None of them compared in scent intensity or performance. This works great in the high heat of summer and lasts for 6-8 hours on the skin in that weather. It's expensive and honestly, I think any perfume over $200 is overpriced, but get it off season on a discount once the hype has died down.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I wore it with an orange dress today and felt like the juiciest yummiest mango there was.<br />
<br />
It is very feminine and sweet on me, the mango note is very realistic but overall its a sweeter fragrance as opposed to a solely photorealistic mango- its more like what mango tastes like than what an unadulterated mango smells like.<br />
<br />
The scent is not linear though; while the essence remains the same, the set down is definitely distinct to the initial spray. However, this is only noticeable when you are reapplying and get a new whiff of the initial fragrance as it will retain the mango vibe regardless of the time from initial spray.<br />
<br />
The longevity is great (I'd say 8 hours) and the sillage will be moderate until the very end where it becomes more intimate.<br />
<br />
Judging by the discrepancies in reviews, this requires sampling before purchasing as it is reliant on skin chemistry and personal preference.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It‚Äôs not really what I‚Äôm looking for, but maybe you are looking for a spicy, woody mango fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="1873600"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=1873600#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1871425" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1536582">Isabellagd</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-16">06/16/23 09:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is an outstanding, totally addictive summer fragrance! It's very sweet, but not cloying, fruity and perfect for hot weather, but not at all similar to the typical tropical summer scents you find everywhere. <br />
<br />
The mango note in God Of Fire - which I'm sure is what everyone's excited about - is very realistic and stays put throughout the wear of the fragrance, which surprised me as I expected it to disappear as I got to the dry down. Longevity on me was really good, around 6-8 hours with very good projection. <br />
<br />
Before I bought this I heard a lot of comparisons with Baccarat Rouge 540, especially the dry down. Personally, I don't see it. Everyone's skin is different but on me, God of Fire a sweet, tropical, slightly woody fragrance, the only similarity I could think of with BR540 is the airiness. To me they're very different in the dry down. <br />
<br />
Compared to Xerjoff's Cruz Del Sur II, this is definitely more refined, more unique and the mango note lasts a lot longer. To me, the mango in God of Fire is more sweet and almost overripe, in Cruz del Sur II is more fresh and juicy, but it doesn't last as long.<br />
<br />
I would definitely recommend sampling this one, it's a beautiful fragrance that I'll be wearing a lot in the summer, but it's definitely not blind-buy safe.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Scent bar is a lovely place to get a sample and/or through luckyscent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="1855577"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=1855577#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1855309" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This is fruity, sweet nice blend for summertime but a little bit synthetic compared to Mango in Mango Kiss. All nice notes doesn‚Äôt come out at all and this stays quite ‚Äúflat‚Äù and boring. Since I already have Mango Kiss I think this is redundant especially because this fruity vibe doesn‚Äôt even last in this. If the middle and base would be strong and complex enough it wouldn‚Äôt matter but now‚Ä¶ just meh. This has woody notes and should be even Oud in the base but in the drydown this scent has changed into a soft skin scent and there is not so much left.<br />
<br />
I was waiting a lot from this scent. That kind of fruity scents like Mango Kiss are not my favourites even if I love it. I love and adore different kind of fruits in perfumes but perfumes which are only fruity scents are boring. I will revisit my sample and check if something has changed.<br />
<br />
EDIT after revisiting:<br />
<br />
What comes to this scent technically, my thoughts are somewhat same, but otherwise my feelings about it has changed.<br />
<br />
This is very soft and creamy Mango in the blend of light woods, Jasmine and Musk. Still a bit synthtetic but not so much. Those notes are the most noticeable and other notes stay muted. There is no Oud in this nor typical smell of Nagarmotha. I can‚Äôt call the base ambery either. I‚Äôm quite surprised now while wearing this since my thoughts differ a lot from what I was thinking one year ago. I think I was just so disappointed in the simplicity of this blend, I was thinking something much more complex. In the same time I was so excited of Mango note in Mango Kiss. Despite all of that, I‚Äôm not juicy fruity girl, which Mango Kiss offers. So I need to take back my words and admit that this is not redundant at all if you have Mango Kiss. Honestly, this is much more me, despite of non existent complex base, and would be happy to wear this one, absolutely more than Mango Kiss. The blend is very linear but  beautiful regardless. It doesn‚Äôt have so much projection nor sillage but not all the scents need to be like that. Actually now while smelling my wrist over and over again this reminds me of "A | Pantheon" which I love so much. It has as well a creamy, soft texture with Mango. Need to compare these two side by side. Need to consider if I have to add this into my wishlist.<br />
<br />
Thank you for reading and I would appreciate if you follow me IG @ninamariah_perfumes</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="1843427"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=1843427#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1842366" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I can also detect some ginger. In my opinion, this fragrance is more feminine than masculine.<br />

Fresh, and not too sweet. Feels a bit tropical. <br />
<br />
I was expecting it to be a bit muddy smelling from the cypriol and oud but they are well behaved.<br />
<br />
This is a nice unisex summertime fragrance. I really don't understand why people are saying it's feminine. It's not all that sweet to my nose. It certainly doesn't have any note in it that pushes it overwhelmingly feminine. <br />
<br />
I can see why there are some comparisons to BR540, the amber note in the base smells similar to BR540. It's likely got some ambroxan. Imagine BR540 with citrus and mango and you've more or less got this fragrance.<br />
<br />
I enjoy this fragrance but given the SHL pricetag i'll probably pass on it. It's pleasant but nothing groundbreaking for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="1809044"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=1809044#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1807209" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I got my sample from Luckyscent. <br />

Smell: 9 out of 10<br />
Longevity: 8 out of 10<br />
Leans More Feminine<br />

The main note to mention during this phase in this fragrance is indeed the mango but don't think of this as a very sweet mango (kinda like how Cruz Del Sur II is a very sweet and smooth mango) its a bit more sour once the opening fades.<br />
<br />
Then this fragrance totally transitions again after an hour or two to something along the lines of Instant Crush (like that powdery touch)... yeah this fragrance goes on a rollercoaster ride unlike anything I've known... since Mortal Skin perhaps but I would argue this one transitions even more than that. Wow this fragrance and its stages blow my mind, each are very nice. I should also probably mention its hard to detect any tropical vibes in this stage. My review confusing? this fragrance is but in a good way.. very interesting. Give it a try, but over some hours in order to fully appreciate it.<br />
<br />
Edit: Now since I own a full bottle I can honestly say this takes my breath away, I've been trying out fragrances 3x or 4x the price of this fragrance lately and they haven't impressed me as much as this one has. Stunning!<br />
<br />
Would I buy: Full bottle in collection as of 11/07/2022<br />
Recommended: An experience to say the least, one needs to fully sample to understand my review.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72381"comment_id="1569592"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/God-of-Fire-72381.html?ccid=1569592#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1828800" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
